#end

#end

@Wong Chung Bang
#end
:touch
#play sexggxeexgxgxax-a
#zap touch
:touch
Ah, greetings, sir. What do you want to
know?

!a; What's going on?
!b; What does "LV" mean?
!c; What are the Relic slots?
!d; Why can't I get more health/ammo?
!e; What's the Score counter used for?
!f; When I pick up ammo, I don't get any.
!g; What is "Weap"?

!table; Experience Table
#end
:a
The point of this game is to upgrade your
character and defeat enemies and Bosses.
The town, where you are now, is the best
place to buy weapons and items. You can
also be healed here, for a price. To the
North is the entrance to a cave, with
other dungeons leading off from it.
#end
:b
"LV" is short for Level. You go up Levels
by getting experience points. You can get
these by defeating enemies and bosses in
dungeons. You also get experience by
finding treasures.
#end
:c
Relics are special items that allow you to
have different skills. You'll already have
one, as you were asked to choose one when
you started the game. Which relic you
chose affects how you progress through the
game, but you'll collect them all
eventually.
#end
:d
If you've tried to get more of an item
(e.g. Ammo) and found you couldn't, it's
because your maximum stats are determined
by your Level. Once you have Levelled up,
your maximum capacities will increase:

:table
Level  Health  Ammo  Torches Exp to LV Up
  1     100     20      5        1000
  2     200     40     10        2000
  3     300     60     15        3000
  4     400     80     20        4000
  5     500    100     25        5000
  6     600    120     30        6000
  7     700    140     35        7000
  8     800    160     40        8000
  9     900    180     45        9000
  A    1000    200     50        ----

There is never any limit to the amount of
Gems that you can carry.
#end
:e
The Score counter is your Experience.
Experience is a measure of your skill in
combat. Once you have enough Experience,
your Level will increase and your maximum
capacities for health, ammo and torches
will increase along with it.
#end
:f
That means you don't have a gun yet.
Upgrade your weapon to at least Level 3
at the Weapon store.
#end
:g
"Weap" is your Weapon Level. As the game
progresses, you can upgrade your weapon to
better models. You start off with just a
knife, but you get a pistol at Level 3.
#end
